when you say she's a programmer , she did do some , but the real thing is to have said the future is going to be much , much more than this .	當你說她是個程式設計師 , 她確實做過 , 但真正的事就是說 , 她做了一些事 , 但真正的事是 , 未來將會變得更多 。
now , a hundred years later , this guy comes along , alan turing , and in 1936 , and invents the computer all over again .	一百年後 , 在1936年後 , 一百年後 , 一百年後 , 一百年後 , 發明了電腦 。
now , of course , babbage's machine was entirely mechanical .	當然 , babbage的機器完全機械 。
turing's machine was entirely theoretical .	turs機器是完全不可思議的 。
both of these guys were coming from a mathematical perspective , but turing told us something very important .	這些人從數學角度來看 , 但卻告訴我們一個非常重要的 。
he laid down the mathematical foundations for computer science , and said , " it doesn't matter how you make a computer . "	他在電腦科學的基礎上 , 說: 「 不論你怎麼做電腦 。 」
it doesn't matter if your computer's mechanical , like babbage's was , or electronic , like computers are today , or perhaps in the future , cells , or , again , mechanical again , once we get into nanotechnology .	不論你的電腦是機械的 , 像是babbage , 或電子 , 如今日 , 電腦的機械 , 或電子 , 如今日 , 電腦的機械 , 可能是未來的 , 或電子 , 如今日 , 或電子 , 只要我們進入奈米科技 。
we could go back to babbage's machine and just make it tiny . all those things are computers .	我們可以回到babbage的機器 , 所有這些東西都是電腦 。
there is in a sense a computing essence .	這裡有一套計算機率 。
this is called the church–turing thesis .	這叫做教堂教堂 。
and so suddenly , you get this link where you say this thing babbage had built really was a computer .	突然間 , 你得到了這個連結 , 說: 「 電腦 」 其實是電腦 。
in fact , it was capable of doing everything we do today with computers , only really slowly .	事實上 , 現今我們用電腦做的事 , 只有非常慢 。
to give you an idea of how slowly , it had about 1k of memory .	為了給你一個想法 , 關於慢慢的速度 , 大約有1k記憶 。
it used punch cards , which were being fed in , and it ran about 10 , 000 times slower the first zx81 .	它用punchcads , 它會用punch卡片 , 它會用punch卡片 , 每一萬次 , 大約一萬次 。
it did have a ram pack .	它有了一支筆電 。
you could add on a lot of extra memory if you wanted to .	你可以加上更多的記憶 , 如果你想要的話 。
so , where does that bring us today ?	所以 , 今天我們來到哪裡呢 ?
so there are plans .	這裡有一些計畫 。
over in swindon , the science museum archives , there are hundreds of plans and thousands of pages of notes written by charles babbage about this analytical engine .	在瑞典 , 科學博物館 , 科學博物館有數以千計的文章 , 科學博物館 , 有數以千計的文章 。
one of those is a set of plans that we call plan 28 , and that is also the name of a charity that i started with doron swade , who was the curator of computing at the science museum , and also the person who drove the project to build a difference engine , and our plan is to build it .	其中一個是我們稱之為 「 計畫 」 的名字 , 也是我在科學博物館的名字 , 他是 「 設計師 」 的名字 , 也是我在科學博物館的名字 , 他也是 「 設計 」 的名字 , 我們稱之為 「 計劃 」 的計畫 , 而我們稱之為 「 計劃 」 的計畫 , 而我們稱之為 「 計劃 」 。
here in south kensington , we will build the analytical engine .	在南肯斯頓 , 我們會建造一個分析引擎 。
the project has a number of parts to it .	專案計畫有幾個部分 。
one was the scanning of babbage's archive .	一個是babbage的掃描 。
that's been done . the second is now the study of all of those plans to determine what to build .	這已經完成了 , 第二個研究是這些計畫的研究 , 來決定該如何建造 。
the third part is a computer simulation of that machine , and the last part is to physically build it at the science museum .	第三部分是電腦模擬 , 最後一部分是電腦模擬 , 最後一部分是電腦模擬 , 最後一部分是電腦模擬 , 最後一部分是實在科學博物館 。
when it's built , you'll finally be able to understand how a computer works , because rather than having a tiny chip in front of you , you've got to look at this humongous thing and say , " ah , i see the memory operating , i see the cpu operating , i hear it operating . i probably smell it operating . "	當它運作時 , 你就得了解電腦如何運作 , 因為在你面前 , 你就得了解電腦工作 , 我聽到它的運作方式 , 我聽到它的動作 , 我聽到它操作 , 我聽到它的動作 , 我聽到它的運作 , 我會聽到它的運作 , 我會聽到它的運作 。
but in between that we're going to do a simulation .	但在我們要做模擬時 , 我們要做模擬 。
babbage himself wrote , he said , as soon as the analytical engine exists , it will surely guide the future course of science .	巴比爾夫寫了 , 他說 , 一旦分析引擎 , 它會確保未來科學的未來 。
of course , he never built it , because he was always fiddling with new plans , but when it did get built , of course , in the 1940s , everything changed .	當然 , 他從來沒有建構它 , 但當它在1940年代時 , 一切都改變了 。
now , i'll just give you a little taste of what it looks like in motion with a video which shows just one part of the cpu mechanism working .	現在 , 我會給你們看一個影片 , 讓你們看看它的樣子 , 像是在動作的一部分 , 一部分是cpu機制工作的一部分 。
so this is just three sets of cogs , and it's going to add . this is the adding mechanism in action , so you imagine this gigantic machine .	這只是三個組合 , 你想像這個巨大的機器 。
so , give me five years .	所以 , 給我五年 。
before the 2030s happen , we'll have it .	在2030年代 , 我們就有了 。
thank you very much .	謝謝大家 。

in this accessible talk from tedxboston , richard resnick shows how cheap and fast genome sequencing is about to turn health care upside down .	在tedxboston , chardrestxboston , chardrestxboston , chardreston , 理查•安德斯頓 , 理查•安德斯頓 , 理查•安德斯頓 , 理查•安德斯頓 , 將健康照護
dna , biotech , health care , science , technology	dna、醫療照護、科學、技術 。
richard resnick: welcome to the genomic revolution	克里斯尼克:歡迎到基因組革命 。
ladies and gentlemen , i present to you the human genome .	各位先生女士 , 我現在給各位看人類基因組 。
chromosome one , top left .	染色體 , 左邊 。
bottom right are the sex chromosomes .	底部是性染色體 。
women have two copies of that big x chromosome ; men have the x and , of course , that small copy of the y .	女人有兩個複製品 , 當然 , 那個小型的x染色體x染色體x染色體 。
sorry boys , but it's just a tiny little thing that makes you different .	抱歉男孩 , 但這只是一個小東西 , 讓你不同 。

daniel kraft invents a better way to harvest bone marrow	丹尼爾•克拉克拉ft發明了更好的方法 , 來達尼爾•克拉克拉ft發明了更好的方法 。
so i am a pediatric cancer doctor and stemcell researcher at stanford university where my clinical focus has been bone marrow transplantation .	我在史丹佛大學的醫學研究人員 , 我的臨床專注在史丹佛大學的研究人員 , 是我臨床專注在史丹佛大學的研究人員 。
now , inspired by jill bolte taylor last year , i didn't bring a human brain , but i did bring a liter of bone marrow .	今年 , 我沒有帶出一個人腦 , 但是我把一個人的腦袋帶給一個人的腦袋 。
and bone marrow is actually what we use to save the lives of tens of thousands of patients , most of whom have advanced malignancies like leukemia and lymphoma and some other diseases .	骨髓是我們所使用的數千個病患 , 大部分的患者都能拯救生命的數千名病人 , 還有其他疾病 。
so , a few years ago , i'm doing my transplant fellowship at stanford .	幾年前 , 我在史丹佛大學工作 。
i'm in the operating room . we have bob here , who is a volunteer donor .	我在手術室裡 , 我們有一位志願者 。
we're sending his marrow across the country to save the life of a child with leukemia .	我們把他的火箭送到整個國家 , 拯救孩童的生命 。
so actually how do we harvest this bone marrow ?	所以 , 我們要如何收到這骨髓呢 ?
well we have a whole o . r . team , general anesthesia , nurses , and another doctor across from me .	我們有一個全部的醫生 , 包括麻醉、護士、護士 , 還有其他醫生 。
bob's on the table , and we take this sort of small needle , you know , not too big .	在桌子上 , 我們拿著這個小小的針頭 , 不太大 。
and the way we do this is we basically place this through the soft tissue , and kind of punch it into the hard bone , into the tuchus that's a technical term and aspirate about 10 mls of bone marrow out , each time , with a syringe .	我們所做的就是 , 把這個軟體組織組合起來 , 將它轉變成骨頭骨髓 , 每次 , 每次 , 大約有十個骨髓 , 將它轉化為骨髓 。
and hand it off to the nurse . she squirts it into a tin .	把它帶進一塊土地上 , 把它帶進一塊土地上 。
hands it back to me . and we do that again and again .	再一次 , 我們再次再次重複它 。
about 200 times usually .	大約200倍 。
and by the end of this my arm is sore , i've got a callus on my hand , let alone bob , whose rear end looks something more like this , like swiss cheese .	最後 , 我的手臂上 , 最後 , 像瑞士一樣 , 像瑞士斯•艾瑞士一樣 。
so i'm thinking , you know , this procedure hasn't changed in about 40 years .	所以 , 我在想 , 你知道嗎 , 這項手術已經沒有改變了40年 。
and there is probably a better way to do this .	或許有更好的方法來做 。
so i thought of a minimally invasive approach , and a new device that we call the marrow miner .	於是我想到了一個新的裝置 , 我們稱之為 「 火箭 」 的新裝置 。
and the marrow miner , the way it works is shown here .	而火箭礦工 , 它的運作方式就是這樣 。
our standard seethrough patient .	我們標準的病人 。
instead of entering the bone dozens of times , we enter just once , into the front of the hip or the back of the hip .	不是再次進一步 , 我們進入了前面的前面 , 進入骨頭的前面 , 再次進入前面 , 進入骨頭的前面 。
and we have a flexible , powered catheter with a special wire loop tip that stays inside the crunchy part of the marrow and follows the contours of the hip , as it moves around .	我們有彈性 , 用一個特殊的線路線路線 , 讓它繞著它移動 。
so it enables you to very rapidly aspirate , or suck out , rich bone marrow very quickly through one hole .	所以它可以讓你快速快速地跳動 , 或很快的 , 很快就在一個洞裡 。
we can do multiple passes through that same entry .	我們能通過相同的熱情來做多次 。
and , so , very quickly , bob can just get one puncture , local anesthesia , and do this harvest as an outpatient .	所以 , 很快地 , 馬鈴薯會成為一個專業、當地的麻醉劑 , 讓它變得很快 。
so i did a few prototypes . i got a small little grant at stanford .	所以我做了幾個原型 , 我在史丹佛大學 。
and played around with this a little bit .	用這一點點來玩 。
and our team members developed this technology .	我們的團隊成員開發了這項技術 。
and eventually we got two large animals , and pig studies .	最後我們有兩個大型動物 , 和豬研究 。
and we found , to our surprise , that we not only got bone marrow out , but we got 10 times the stem cell activity in the marrow from the marrow miner , compared to the normal device .	我們發現 , 對於一般裝置來說 , 我們發現的 , 不只是骨頭骨髓 , 而是有10倍的幹細胞活動 , 讓骨髓移植 , 更為正常的裝置 。
this device was just fda approved in the last year .	這個裝置只是fda應用在過去一年 。
here is a live patient . you can see it following the flexible curves around .	這是個病人 , 你可以看到它在追蹤著有彈性的曲線
there will be two passes here , in the same patient , from the same hole .	這裡有兩個熱帶 , 相同的病人 , 相同的病人 。
this was done under local anesthesia , as an outpatient .	這是在當地的麻醉劑 , 身為獨裁者 。
and we got , again , about three to six times more stem cells than the standard approach done on the same patient .	再一次 , 三到六倍的幹細胞比標準的標準方式更幹細胞 。
so why should you care ? bone marrow is a very rich source of adult stem cells .	所以 , 你為什麼要關心 ? 骨髓是一個非常豐富的成年人幹細胞 。
you all know about embryonic stem cells .	你們都知道胚胎幹細胞 。
they've got great potential but haven't yet entered clinical trials .	他們有很棒的潛力 , 但沒有進入臨床試驗 。
adult stem cells are throughout our body , including the bloodforming stem cells in our bone marrow , which we've been using as a form of stemcell therapy for over 40 years .	成年人幹細胞在我們的骨髓中幹細胞 , 包括在我們的骨髓中幹細胞 , 包括在我們的骨髓中幹細胞 , 包含了40年來的幹細胞 。
in the last decade there's been an explosion of use of bone marrow stem cells to treat the patient's other diseases such as heart disease , vascular disease , orthopedics , tissue engineering , even in neurology to treat parkinson's and diabetes .	在過去的幾十年內 , 由骨髓幹細胞來治療病人的其他疾病 , 像是心臟病、血管、骨髓幹細胞 , 及糖尿病 。
we've just come out , we're commercializing , this year , generation 2 . 0 of the marrow miner .	我們剛剛出去了 , 今年 , 一代2.0.0.0.
the hope is that this gets more stem cells out , which translates to better outcomes .	希望是 , 使得更好的收入更好的結果 。
it may encourage more people to sign up to be potential livesaving bone marrow donors .	可能鼓勵更多人來追求潛力的骨髓捐贈者 。
it may even enable you to bank your own marrow stem cells , when you're younger and healthier , to use in the future should you need it .	甚至可以讓你能在未來你需要它 , 讓你能在未來你需要它 。
and ultimately and here's a picture of our bone marrow transplant survivors , who come together for a reunion each year at stanford .	最後 , 這是我們骨髓移植手術的照片 , 每一年都在史丹佛 。
hopefully this technology will let us have more of these survivors in the future .	希望這項科技能讓我們有更多的生存者 。
physicist and surfer garrett lisi presents a controversial new model of the universe that just maybe answers all the big questions . if nothing else , it's the most beautiful 8dimensional model of elementary particles and forces you've ever seen .	物理學家 , 物理學家 , 物理學家 , 物理學家 , 物理學家 , 物理學家 , 物理學家 , 和你所見過的宇宙中最美妙的圖案 , 解釋所有大問題 。 如果沒有其他東西 , 它是最美麗的形式模型 。
physics , science , technology	物理學、科學、科學 。
garrett lisi on his theory of everything	garrettlisi在他的理論上 。
whoa , dude . check out those killer equations . sweet .	誰 , 看看那些殺人的方程式 , 和瑞典 。
actually , for the next 18 minutes i'm going to do the best i can to describe the beauty of particle physics without equations .	事實上 , 接下來的18分鐘 , 我要做的最好 , 我可以描述美麗的粒子物理學 , 不用方程式 。
it turns out there's a lot we can learn from coral .	結果發現 , 我們從珊瑚身上學到很多 。
coral is a very beautiful and unusual animal .	珊瑚是非常美麗且不尋常的動物 。
each coral head consists of thousand of individual polyps .	每個珊瑚頭都有數千個個體 。
these polyps are continually budding and branching into genetically identical neighbors .	這些蜜蜂會被遺傳到基因上的鄰居 。
if we imagine this to be a hyperintelligent coral , we can single out an individual and ask him a reasonable question .	如果我們想像這是個高智力的珊瑚 , 我們可以單單一個個人 , 並問他一個問題 。
we can ask how exactly he got to be in this particular location compared to his neighbors if it was just chance , or destiny , or what ?	我們可以問他如何在這個特定的位置上 , 和他的鄰居一樣 , 不論是哪裡 ?
now , after admonishing us for turning the temperature up too high , he would tell us that our question was completely stupid .	為了讓溫度太高 , 他會告訴我們問題是完全愚蠢的 。
these corals can be quite kind of mean , you see , and i have surfing scars to prove that .	這些珊瑚都可以很有意思 , 我很有害怕去證明它 。
but this polyp would continue and tell us that his neighbors were quite clearly identical copies of him .	但這條詩會繼續告訴我們 , 他的鄰居是非常明顯的同事 。
that he was in all these other locations as well , but experiencing them as separate individuals .	他在其他的位置上 , 都在其他的位置上 , 但在這些其他地方的位置上 , 卻被分離的位置 。
for a coral , branching into different copies is the most natural thing in the world .	對珊瑚而言 , 世界中最自然的東西 。
unlike us , a hyperintelligent coral would be uniquely prepared to understand quantum mechanics .	不如我們所知量子力學 , 一個高級的神經元素 , 很不可思議 。
the mathematics of quantum mechanics very accurately describes how our universe works .	量子力學的數學是量子力學所描述的數學
and it tells us our reality is continually branching into different possibilities , just like a coral .	它告訴我們 , 我們的現實是不斷地擴展到不同的可能性 , 就像珊瑚一樣 。
it's a weird thing for us humans to wrap our minds around , since we only ever get to experience one possibility .	對於人類來說 , 很奇怪的是 , 我們從我們身上學到一個可能性 。
this quantum weirdness was first described by erwin schrödinger and his cat .	這個量子奇怪的第一個描述 , 叫做schrolderwinschroldschr和他的貓 。
the cat likes this version better .	貓喜歡這個版本更好 。
in this setup , schrödinger is in a box with a radioactive sample that , by the laws of quantum mechanics , branches into a state in which it is radiated and a state in which it is not .	在這個組合中 , 法律量子機制定律的量子力學院 , 用量子力學的原理 , 來源於量子力學的狀態 , 不論是在哪裡 。
in the branch in which the sample radiates , it sets off a trigger that releases poison and schrödinger is dead .	在這個樣本中 , 它會釋放出毒品和吸毒劑 , 它會釋放出毒品和呼吸器 。
but in the other branch of reality , he remains alive .	但在其他的情況下 , 他仍然活著 。
these realities are experienced separately by each individual .	這些真實體驗到每個人的體驗 。
as far as either can tell , the other one doesn't exist .	儘管如此 , 其他人也不存在 。
this seems weird to us , because each of us only experiences an individual existence , and we don't get to see other branches .	這對我們來說很奇怪 , 因為我們每個人都只有體驗一個獨立的體驗 , 因為每個人都只有體驗一個獨立的體驗 , 而我們不得不看到其他的偏見 。
it's as if each of us , like schrödinger here , are a kind of coral branching into different possibilities .	像schroldschr一樣 , 每個人都像schrodschr一樣 , 會變成不同的可能性 。
the mathematics of quantum mechanics tells us this is how the world works at tiny scales .	量子力學的數學量子力學告訴我們這個世界是如何運作的 。
it can be summed up in a single sentence: everything that can happen , does .	它可以在一個句子裡:所有事情都能發生 。
but this does not mean everything happens .	但這並不意味著一切發生了 。
the rest of physics is about describing what can happen and what can't .	物理學的描述可能發生了什麼事 , 不該怎麼做 。
what physics tells us is that everything comes down to geometry and the interactions of elementary particles .	物理學告訴我們 , 物理學會告訴我們 , 每件事都在幾何物理學中 , 和互動的互動 。
and things can happen only if these interactions are perfectly balanced .	若這些互動是完美的平衡 。
now i'll go ahead and describe how we know about these particles , what they are and how this balance works .	現在我要向各位解釋我們如何知道這些粒子 , 以及這些粒子如何運作 。
in this machine , a beam of protons and antiprotons are accelerated to near the speed of light and brought together in a collision , producing a burst of pure energy .	在這個機器中 , 大量的光線和光速 , 形成了一顆光子 , 形成了一顆光子 , 形成了一顆光子 , 形成了一顆光子 。
this energy is immediately converted into a spray of subatomic particles , with detectors and computers used to figure out their properties .	這個能量會被轉換成一種噴射性粒子的粒子 , 和電腦用來找出它們的特性 。
this enormous machine the large hadron collider at cern in geneva has a circumference of 17 miles and , when it's operating , draws five times as much power as the city of monterey .	這種巨大的大型鐵粒在盧安達了十七英里 , 當它運作時 , 它的運作方式 , 大約有十七英里 , 同時 , 它的運作方式 , 大約有十七英里 。
we can't predict specifically what particles will be produced in any individual collision .	我們無法預測特定的粒子會在任何一個體內產生 。
quantum mechanics tells us all possibilities are realized .	量子力學告訴我們所有可能性 。
but physics does tell us what particles can be produced .	但物理學告訴我們粒子可以產生什麼粒子 。
these particles must have just as much mass and energy as is carried in by the proton and antiproton .	這些粒子必須有那麼多的能量 , 如同在華盛頓和維羅頓的粒子 。
any particles more massive than this energy limit aren't produced , and remain invisible to us .	任何粒子比這個能量限制更大 , 還不夠大量 , 不管我們怎麼做 。
this is why this new particle accelerator is so exciting .	這就是為什麼這個新粒子加速器非常興奮 。
it's going to push this energy limit seven times beyond what's ever been done before , so we're going to get to see some new particles very soon .	它會將這個能量限七倍以來 , 所以我們將會看到一些新的粒子 。
but before talking about what we might see , let me describe the particles we already know of .	但在談談我們所知道的粒子之前 , 讓我描述我們所知的粒子 。
there's a whole zoo of subatomic particles .	這裡有一整個大粒子 。
most of us are familiar with electrons .	我們大部分人都熟悉電子 。
a lot of people in this room make a good living pushing them around .	許多人在這個房間裡有許多人在這個房間裡 , 讓它們變得好 。
but the electron also has a neutral partner called the neutrino , with no electric charge and a very tiny mass .	但電荷和一個非常小的電荷 , 沒有電荷 , 電荷和一個非常小的電荷 。
in contrast , the upanddown quarks have very large masses , and combine in threes to make the protons and neutrons inside atoms .	相反的 , 大量的原子和中子中間的原子有大量 , 三分之二的原子組成了原子的原子 。
all of these matter particles come in left and righthanded varieties , and have antiparticle partners that carry opposite charges .	所有這些物質粒子都在左邊和右邊的粒子 , 相反的粒子會產生相反的粒子 。
these familiar particles also have less familiar second and third generations , which have the same charges as the first but have much higher masses .	這些熟悉的粒子也比較少熟悉的粒子和第三代 , 相同的頻率也比較少熟悉的粒子 , 相同的頻率也比較少熟悉的粒子 。
these matter particles all interact with the various force particles .	這些物質粒子和不同粒子相互作用 。
the electromagnetic force interacts with electrically charged matter via particles called photons .	電磁力會產生電磁力作用 , 電磁力會產生電磁作用 , 稱為光子 。
there is also a very weak force called , rather unimaginatively , the weak force , that interacts only with lefthanded matter .	還有一種非常弱勢的力量 , 不是想像力、弱勢 , 而不是想像力、弱勢 , 或弱勢的力量 , 只剩下一個很弱的力量 。
the strong force acts between quarks which carry a different kind of charge , called color charge , and come in three different varieties: red , green and blue .	強力的強力作用在三種不同的變形中:紅色、綠色和藍色 。
you can blame murray gellmann for these names they're his fault .	你可以把murraygellmann為這些名字的名字為這些名字 。
finally , there's the force of gravity , which interacts with matter via its mass and spin .	最後 , 重力的力量是重力的力量 , 它的作用力和旋轉 。
the most important thing to understand here is that there's a different kind of charge associated with each of these forces .	最重要的是 , 這裡有一種不同的特徵 , 和這些力量之間的關係 。
these four different forces interact with matter according to the corresponding charges that each particle has .	這四種不同的力量互相交互作用 , 每粒子都有相同的作用 。
a particle that hasn't been seen yet , but we're pretty sure exists , is the higgs particle , which gives masses to all these other particles .	粒子還沒見過 , 但是我們很確定存在 , 希格斯粒子的粒子 , 粒子會產生大量的粒子 。
the main purpose of the large hadron collider is to see this higgs particle , and we're almost certain it will .	大型粒子的主要目的是要看到希格斯粒子 , 我們幾乎一定會這樣 。
but the greatest mystery is what else we might see .	但最偉大的神秘是我們可能看到的 。
and i'm going to show you one beautiful possibility towards the end of this talk .	接下來我要展示一個美麗的可能性 , 來展示一個美麗的可能性 。
now , if we count up all these different particles using their various spins and charges , there are 226 .	現在 , 如果我們把這些不同的粒子用不同粒子組合起來 , 會有226 。
that's a lot of particles to keep track of .	很多粒子可以持續追蹤 。
and it seems strange that nature would have so many elementary particles .	大自然有這麼多元素 。
but if we plot them out according to their charges , some beautiful patterns emerge .	但如果我們把它們排放出來 , 有些美麗的模式就會出現 。
the most familiar charge is electric charge .	最熟悉的電荷是電荷 。
electrons have an electric charge , a negative one , and quarks have electric charges in thirds .	電子電荷有電荷 , 電荷有電荷 , 電荷有電荷 , 電荷有電荷 。
so when two up quarks and a down quark are combined to make a proton , it has a total electric charge of plus one .	所以 , 當兩方平方公平方時 , 它有電荷的電荷 。
these particles also have antiparticles , which have opposite charges .	這些粒子有反粒子 , 反粒子也有反粒子 。
now , it turns out the electric charge is actually a combination of two other charges: hypercharge and weak charge .	事實上 , 電荷有兩個其他荷蘭的結合 , 電荷是兩個其他荷蘭的結合 。
if we spread out the hypercharge and weak charge and plot the charges of particles in this twodimensional charge space , the electric charge is where these particles sit along the vertical direction .	如果我們把這些粒子放在電荷上 , 電荷 , 電荷會把這些粒子放在兩維空間中 , 電荷 , 電荷則是這些粒子在相互作用的方向上 。
the electromagnetic and weak forces interact with matter according to their hypercharge and weak charge , which make this pattern .	電磁和弱力會產生這種模式 。
this is called the unified electroweak model , and it was put together back in 1967 .	這叫做 「 無線電擊模式 」 , 它在1967年被稱為 「 獨立的選舉 」 。
the reason most of us are only familiar with electric charge and not both of these is because of the higgs particle .	我們大部分人都只熟悉電荷 , 而不是這些是因為希格斯粒子 。
the higgs , over here on the left , has a large mass and breaks the symmetry of this electroweak pattern .	希格斯在左邊有個大大的對稱 , 左邊有大量的對稱性 。
it makes the weak force very weak by giving the weak particles a large mass .	它讓弱力弱弱強弱 , 讓弱勢力弱強弱力弱力弱弱 。
since this massive higgs sits along the horizontal direction in this diagram , the photons of electromagnetism remain massless and interact with electric charge along the vertical direction in this charge space .	由於這種巨大的希格斯在這個圖片中 , 電磁鐵路線的光子 , 電磁鐵路線的電路線上 , 電力和電力之間的光子是電磁共振的方向 , 電力和電力之間的相互作用 , 可以維持大量的光子 。
so the electromagnetic and weak forces are described by this pattern of particle charges in twodimensional space .	所以電磁力和弱力在兩個維度空間中產生電磁和弱力 。
we can include the strong force by spreading out its two charge directions and plotting the charges of the force particles in quarks along these directions .	我們能把強力強力推動 , 把強力的電力轉換成兩條荷爾定位 , 將它們的方向推向方向 。
the charges of all known particles can be plotted in a fourdimensional charge space , and projected down to two dimensions like this so we can see them .	所有知識粒子都能在四維空間中 , 把它們放到兩個維度 , 像這樣我們就可以看到它們 。
whenever particles interact , nature keeps things in a perfect balance along all four of these charge directions .	當粒子互相作用時 , 自然保持在完美的平衡中 , 自然總是在四個特定的平衡中 。
if a particle and an antiparticle collide , it creates a burst of energy and a total charge of zero in all four charge directions .	如果粒子和反粒子會產生能量 , 它會產生一顆粒子和抗粒子 , 它會創造出一顆粒子和抗粒子 , 它會創造出一顆粒子和抗粒子 , 它會創造出一顆粒子和抗粒子 , 它會創造出一顆粒子和抗粒子 。
at this point , anything can be created as long as it has the same energy and maintains a total charge of zero .	此時 , 任何東西都可以用同樣的能量和維持電力來維持永續的能量 。
for example , this weak force particle and its antiparticle can be created in a collision .	例如 , 這種弱力粒子和抗粒子可以在撞擊力粒子中形成 。
in further interactions , the charges must always balance .	在外交互相交互作用 , 荷爾必須保持平衡 。
one of the weak particles could decay into an electron and an antineutrino , and these three still add to zero total charge .	一顆粒子可以解放一顆粒子 , 將其三分之一加入電子 , 而這三個仍然加入電子 。
nature always keeps a perfect balance .	自然總是保持完美的平衡 。
so these patterns of charges are not just pretty .	所以這些圖案不僅僅是如此 。
they tell us what interactions are allowed to happen .	他們告訴我們互動是如何互動的 。
and we can rotate this charge space in four dimensions to get a better look at the strong interaction , which has this nice hexagonal symmetry .	我們可以在四維空間中 , 讓它變得更好 , 看看強大的互動 , 這對稱性是對稱的 。
in a strong interaction , a strong force particle , such as this one , interacts with a colored quark , such as this green one , to give a quark with a different color charge this red one .	在強烈的作用中 , 強力粒子的作用 , 比如這個綠色 , 一個強大的粒子 , 例如這個綠色 , 一個強力粒子 , 例如這個紅色 。
and strong interactions are happening millions of times each second in every atom of our bodies , holding the atomic nuclei together .	強大的作用在我們身體中每秒鐘的每秒鐘內 , 每秒鐘都在我們的身體中 , 形成原子核心 。
but these four charges corresponding to three forces are not the end of the story .	但這四個章節 , 不是故事的四個章節 。
we can also include two more charges corresponding to the gravitational force .	我們也能將兩條線索轉換為重力 。
when we include these , each matter particle has two different spin charges , spinup and spindown .	當我們把這些物質粒子結合在一起時 , 每個物質粒子都有兩種不同的旋轉和旋轉 。
so they all split , and give a nice pattern in sixdimensional charge space .	所以它們都在六維空間中提供一個很好的圖案
we can rotate this pattern in six dimensions , and see that it's quite pretty .	我們可以把這個模式放在六維空間中 , 看到它非常非常 。
right now , this pattern matches our best current knowledge of how nature is built at the tiny scales of these elementary particles .	現在 , 這種圖案在我們最好的知識中 , 了解自然如何建立在這些元素的大自然中 。
this is what we know for certain .	這是我們所知道的 。
some of these particles are at the very limit of what we've been able to reach with experiments .	有些粒子是非常有限的 , 我們能夠達到實驗 。
from this pattern , we already know the particle physics of these tiny scales . the way the universe works with these tiny scales is very beautiful .	從這個模式中 , 我們已經知道粒子物理的粒子物理 , 這些小小的尺度是非常美麗的 。
but now i'm going to discuss some new and old ideas about things we don't know yet .	但現在我要討論一些新和舊的想法 , 我們不知道 。
we want to expand this pattern using mathematics alone , and see if we can get our hands on the whole enchilada .	我們想要擴展這個模式 , 看看如果我們能把我們的手放在全部的圖案中 。
we want to find all the particles and forces that make a complete picture of our universe .	我們想要找到所有的粒子和力量 , 使我們宇宙中的所有粒子 。
and we want to use this picture to predict new particles that we'll see when experiments reach higher energies .	我們想要用這張圖來預測新的粒子 , 我們想用這張圖來預測新的粒子 , 來預測新的粒子 , 來預測新的粒子 。
so there's an old idea in particle physics that this known pattern of charges , which is not very symmetric , could emerge from a more perfect pattern that gets broken similar to how the higgs particle breaks the electroweak pattern to give electromagnetism .	在粒子物理中 , 粒子物理學的圖案是對稱的 , 不是非常正確的 , 可以從一個更完美的圖案中 , 讓電磁共振的圖案 , 讓電磁力產生的電磁性 。
in order to do this , we need to introduce new forces with new charge directions .	為了做到這一點 , 我們需要介紹新荷蘭的新載荷 。
when we introduce a new direction , we get to guess what charges the particles have along this direction , and then we can rotate it in with the others .	當我們引導一個新的方向時 , 我們會把這些粒子帶到另一個方向 , 然後我們將它帶到另一個方向 。
if we guess wisely , we can construct the standard charges in six charge dimensions as a broken symmetry of this more perfect pattern in seven charge dimensions .	如果我們猜測量 , 我們就能建構標準的標準標準 , 用六個荷蘭的標準標準 , 將標準的標準標準放在六個載荷的標準目標中 , 將標準的標準目標放在六個荷爾的標準目標中 。
this particular choice corresponds to a grand unified theory introduced by pati and salam in 1973 .	這種特定的選擇回應在1973年的奧斯塔亞和薩爾姆 。
when we look at this new unified pattern , we can see a couple of gaps where particles seem to be missing .	當我們觀察這個新發現的模式時 , 我們可以看到一些小粒子似乎失敗了 。
this is the way theories of unification work .	這是一種理論的理論 。
a physicist looks for larger , more symmetric patterns that include the established pattern as a subset .	物理學家看起來更大 , 更大的 , 更大的模式 , 包括建立模式的模式 。
the larger pattern allows us to predict the existence of particles that have never been seen .	更大的模式讓我們能預測宇宙的粒子從未見過的 。
this unification model predicts the existence of these two new force particles , which should act a lot like the weak force , only weaker .	這個模型預測了這兩個新粒子的存在 , 它應該要像弱勢一樣 , 更像弱勢力 , 只是弱勢 。
now we can rotate this set of charges in seven dimensions and consider an odd fact about the matter particles: the second and third generations of matter have exactly the same charges in sixdimensional charge space as the first generation .	現在我們可以在六維空間中做出相同的載荷 , 在七度空間中 , 將這組成分為第一代 。
these particles are not uniquely identified by their six charges .	這些粒子並不是獨特的六個特徵 。
they sit on top of one another in the standard charge space .	他們坐在標準的旁邊 。
however , if we work in eightdimensional charge space , then we can assign unique new charges to each particle .	然而 , 如果我們在八度空間中 , 我們就可以把獨特的新荷蘭送給每個粒子 。
then we can spin these in eight dimensions , and see what the whole pattern looks like .	然後 , 看看整個模式的樣子是什麼樣子 。
here we can see the second and third generations of matter now related to the first generation by a symmetry called " triality . "	這裡我們可以看到第二個第三代 , 與第一代有關聯繫 , 稱之為 「 試驗 」 。
this particular pattern of charges in eight dimensions is actually part of the most beautiful geometric structure in mathematics .	這個特定的圖案是數學中最美麗的幾何結構之一 。
it's a pattern of the largest exceptional lie group , e8 .	這是最大型的圖案之一 , 8歲 。
this lie group is a smooth , curved shape with 248 dimensions .	這隻獅子是一顆滑鼠 , 兩個48維度的形狀 。
each point in this pattern corresponds to a symmetry of this very complex and beautiful shape .	這個模式對稱的對稱是非常複雜且美麗的形狀 。
one small part of this e8 shape can be used to describe the curved spacetime of einstein's general relativity , explaining gravity .	八形形狀的一小部分 , 可以用來描述 「 愛因斯坦公平 」 的一小部分 , 解釋重力 。
together with quantum mechanics , the geometry of this shape could describe everything about how the universe works at the tiniest scales .	用量子力學來描述所有關於宇宙如何運作的幾何形狀
the pattern of this shape living in eightdimensional charge space is exquisitely beautiful , and it summarizes thousands of possible interactions between these elementary particles , each of which is just a facet of this complicated shape .	這種形狀的形狀存在於八維空間的形狀中 , 這種形狀的形狀是非常美麗的 , 而它在八維空間之間的形狀是非常美麗的 , 每一部分都只是一個複雜的形狀 。
as we spin it , we can see many of the other intricate patterns contained in this one .	隨著我們加入它 , 我們可以看到許多其他的圖案在這個過程中 。
and with a particular rotation , we can look down through this pattern in eight dimensions along a symmetry axis and see all the particles at once .	順便一提 , 我們可以看到所有的粒子在一個特定的位置中 , 以一個特定的角度來觀察這個模式 。
it's a very beautiful object , and as with any unification , we can see some holes where new particles are required by this pattern .	它是一個非常美麗的物體 , 我們可以看到一些洞見到新粒子的物體 。
there are 20 gaps where new particles should be , two of which have been filled by the patisalam particles .	新粒子有20個葡萄 , 可能有20個葡萄 , 粒子應該有兩種 。
from their location in this pattern , we know that these new particles should be scalar fields like the higgs particle , but have color charge and interact with the strong force .	在這個圖案中 , 我們知道這些新粒子應該是像希格斯粒子一樣 , 但有顏色和強力的作用 。
filling in these new particles completes this pattern , giving us the full e8 .	在這些新粒子中 , 給予我們全部的8 。
this e8 pattern has very deep mathematical roots .	這8個模式有非常深的數學根源 。
it's considered by many to be the most beautiful structure in mathematics .	它被認為是數學中最美麗的結構 。
it's a fantastic prospect that this object of great mathematical beauty could describe the truth of particle interactions at the smallest scales imaginable .	這是個很棒的數學美麗 , 可以描述在最小的尺度中 , 可以描述出真相的真相 。
and this idea that nature is described by mathematics is not at all new .	而這個想法 , 大自然被數學不是全新的 。
in 1623 , galileo wrote this: " nature's grand book , which stands continually open to our gaze , is written in the language of mathematics .	在1623年 , 在1623年 , 蓋爾文寫了 「 大自然的書 」 , 寫著 「 大自然的書 」 , 寫著 「 大自然 」 的書 , 寫著 「 大自然 」 的語言 。
its characters are triangles , circles and other geometrical figures , without which it is humanly impossible to understand a single word of it ; without these , one is wandering around in a dark labyrinth . "	它的角色是三角形、圓圈和其他幾何圖形 , 不論是人類無法理解一個字 , 沒有任何一個字 , 它的角色是三角形、圓圈和其他幾何形式 。 」
i believe this to be true , and i've tried to follow galileo's guidance in describing the mathematics of particle physics using only triangles , circles and other geometrical figures .	我相信這是真的 , 我一直在描述數學的粒子物理學 , 用三角形、圓形和其他幾何形式來描述數學 。
of course , when other physicists and i actually work on this stuff , the mathematics can resemble a dark labyrinth .	當然 , 其他物理學家 , 我真的在研究這個東西 , 數學可以重新組成一個黑暗的實驗室 。
but it's reassuring that at the heart of this mathematics is pure , beautiful geometry .	但在這個數學的心中 , 美麗的幾何形式是純粹的 。
joined with quantum mechanics , this mathematics describes our universe as a growing e8 coral , with particles interacting at every location in all possible ways according to a beautiful pattern .	加入量子力學 , 用量子力學來描述我們的宇宙 , 一個美麗的圖案 , 和量子力學所描述的 , 相互作用 。
and as more of the pattern comes into view using new machines like the large hadron collider , we may be able to see whether nature uses this e8 pattern or a different one .	隨著圖像大型的新機器 , 我們可能可以看到大自然使用的新機器 , 像是大型的新機器 , 我們可能可以看到 , 大自然使用的新機器 , 像是大型的新機器 。
this process of discovery is a wonderful adventure to be involved in .	這個過程發現了一種很棒的冒險 。
if the lhc finds particles that fit this e8 pattern , that will be very , very cool .	如果lhc發現粒子的粒子 , 它會非常酷 。
if the lhc finds new particles , but they don't fit this pattern well , that will be very interesting , but bad for this e8 theory .	如果lhc發現新粒子 , 但它們不符合這個模式 , 但它們不符合這個模式 , 會很有趣 , 但它們不符合這類型態的新粒子 。
and , of course , bad for me personally .	當然 , 對我個人來說 , 很糟糕 。
now how bad would that be ?	那會是多麼糟糕的 ?
well , pretty bad .	嗯 , 很糟 。
but predicting how nature works is a very risky game .	但預測大自然的運作是非常危險的遊戲 。
this theory and others like it are long shots .	這種理論和其他類似的東西很長 。
one does a lot of hard work knowing that most of these ideas probably won't end up being true about nature .	其中一個非常困難的研究 , 大部分的點子可能不會終於自然界 。
that's what doing theoretical physics is like: there are a lot of wipeouts .	這就是理論物理的理論物理:有許多野生 。
in this regard , new physics theories are a lot like startup companies .	在這個領域中 , 新物理理論就像創作公司 。
as with any large investment , it can be emotionally difficult to abandon a line of research when it isn't working out .	隨著任何大的投資 , 它可以很困難 , 可以在工作時 , 都無法處理 。
but in science , if something isn't working , you have to toss it out and try something else .	但在科學上 , 如果你沒有工作 , 你必須去嘗試其他東西 。
now , the only way to maintain sanity and achieve happiness in the midst of this uncertainty is to keep balance and perspective in life .	現在 , 唯一能維持平衡和觀念的唯一方式就是保持平衡和觀念 。
i've tried the best i can to live a balanced life .	我曾嘗試過最好的生命 , 可以活得平衡 。
i try to balance my life equally between physics , love and surfing my own three charge directions .	我試著平衡我的人生平衡 , 愛 , 和我的三項目擊 。
this way , even if the physics i work on comes to nothing , i still know i've lived a good life .	這種方式 , 即使物理學的物理 , 我仍然知道我工作的物理是好的 。
and i try to live in beautiful places .	我試著住在美麗的地方 。
for most of the past ten years i've lived on the island of maui , a very beautiful place .	過去十年來 , 我住在島上 , 非常美麗的地方 。
now it's one of the greatest mysteries in the universe to my parents how i managed to survive all that time without engaging in anything resembling fulltime employment .	這是我最偉大的謎題之一 , 是我父母們 , 我能在任何一生中都沒有參與其中一件事 。
i'm going to let you in on that secret .	我要讓你們在秘密上 。
this was a view from my home office on maui .	這是我家辦公室的一場景象 。
and you may have noticed that these beautiful views are similar , but in slightly different places .	你可能注意到這些美麗的觀點是相似的 , 但在不同的地方 。
that's because this used to be my home and office on maui .	這是因為這習慣於我家和辦公室 。

living a nomadic existence has been hard at times , but it's allowed me to live in beautiful places and keep a balance in my life that i've been happy with .	生活在美麗的平衡中 , 它讓我活在美麗的地方 , 並保持平衡 , 讓我生活在美麗的地方 , 並且保持平衡的平衡 。

it's kind of commonplace now , but his argument was because he'd been searching for the fossilized remains of early humans in africa .	這很普遍 , 但他的爭論是 , 因為他在非洲的早期被搜尋了 。
and you can tell an awful lot about what those beings looked like from the fossils , from the shape of the muscle attachments , something about the way they lived from the various artifacts found with them .	你可以從各式各樣的角度來看 , 像是從石頭上看來的 , 從石頭的角度來看 , 它們從各樣各樣的形狀 , 來源自於各種藝術品的樣子 。
but what about how they behaved ? that's what he wanted to know .	但他們是怎樣的呢 ? 這就是他想要知道的 。
and of course , behavior doesn't fossilize .	當然 , 行為不會化 。
he argued and it's now a fairly common theory that if we found behavior patterns similar or the same in our closest living relatives , the great apes , and humans today , then maybe those behaviors were present in the apelike , humanlike ancestor some seven million years ago .	他認為 , 如果我們發現行為模式相似或相同的相似 , 人類的祖先 , 人類的祖先 , 可能是人類的祖先 , 大約有七百萬年前 。
and therefore , perhaps we had brought those characteristics with us from that ancient , ancient past .	因此 , 也許我們從古老的古老人身上學到了這些特徵 。
well , if you look in textbooks today that deal with human evolution , you very often find people speculating about how early humans may have behaved , based on the behavior of chimpanzees .	嗯 , 如果你看看現今的人類演化 , 你通常會發現人類演化的行為 , 尤其是在黑猩猩的行為中 。
they are more like us than any other living creature , and we've heard about that during this ted conference .	他們比其他生物更像我們 , 我們都聽過這場ted會議 。
so it remains for me to comment on the ways in which chimpanzees are so like us , in certain aspects of their behavior .	所以 , 我對這些黑猩猩的角度來說 , 對我來說 , 那些黑猩猩對我們來說 , 對我來說 , 那些黑猩猩的角度是如此 。
every chimpanzee has his or her own personality .	每個黑猩猩都有自己的個人性 。
of course , i gave them names . they can live to be 60 years or more , although we think most of them probably don't make it to 60 in the wild .	當然 , 我給他們名字 , 儘管我們認為大多數人可能不用六十歲 , 儘管我們認為大部分的人都可能不會在野生上60歲 。
mr . wurzel . the female has her first baby when she's 11 or 12 .	mr.wurzel , 她的第一個嬰兒在11或12歲時 。
thereafter , she has one baby only every five or six years , a long period of childhood dependency when the child is nursing , sleeping with the mother at night , and riding on her back .	每五或六年 , 每五或六年來 , 孩子們都在睡眠 , 媽媽在晚上 , 和母親在晚上 , 她的孩子很長時間 , 孩子們都在睡眠 , 和母親在晚上 , 和母親一起回來 。
and we believe that this long period of childhood is important for chimpanzees , just as it is for us , in relation to learning .	我們相信 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 對於黑猩猩而言 , 我們相信這長期是很重要的 。
as the brain becomes ever more complex during evolution in different forms of animals , so we find that learning plays an ever more important role in an individual's life history .	隨著大腦變得更複雜 , 在演化中 , 我們發現學習扮演了更重要的角色 , 在演化中 , 人類的生命歷史中扮演了重要的角色 。
and young chimpanzees spend a lot of time watching what their elders do .	年輕黑猩猩花了很多時間看著他們的老虎 。
we know now that they're capable of imitating behaviors that they see .	我們現在知道他們能否認他們所看到的行為 。
and we believe that it's in this way that the different toolusing behaviors that have now been seen in all the different chimpanzee populations studied in africa how these are passed from one generation to the next , through observation , imitation and practice , so that we can describe these toolusing behaviors as primitive culture .	我們相信 , 透過觀察、觀念和行為 , 我們相信 , 透過觀察、觀念和行為 , 我們相信 , 透過觀察、觀察、承認和行為 , 我們相信 , 透過觀察者的行為 , 我們相信 , 這種方式 , 透過觀察者的行為 , 透過觀察者 , 來描述這些工具的行為 , 以至今日 , 世界各地都被視為原始文化 。
chimpanzees don't have a spoken language . we've talked about that .	黑猩猩不會有一種語言 , 我們已經談過了 。
they do have a very rich repertoire of postures and gestures , many of which are similar , or even identical , to ours and formed in the same context . greeting chimpanzees embracing .	他們有非常豐富的重複性 , 或同情心 , 甚至是同類的 , 甚至是相同的 , 甚至是同類的 , 甚至是同類的 , 甚至是同類的 , 甚至是同類的 , 甚至是同情心的 , 或甚至是同情形的 , 也是相同的 。
they also kiss , hold hands , pat one another on the back .	他們也能用手 , 拿手 , 把手放在背後 。
and they swagger and they throw rocks .	牠們會游泳 , 把石頭丟掉 。
in chimpanzee society , we find many , many examples of compassion , precursors to love and true altruism .	在黑猩猩社會中 , 我們發現很多許多例子 , 像是同情心、愛情和真實的愛情 。
unfortunately , they , like us , have a dark side to their nature .	不幸的是 , 他們就像我們一樣 , 他們喜歡我們 , 他們和我們一樣有黑暗面 。
they're capable of extreme brutality , even a kind of primitive war .	它們是極端的殘酷 , 甚至是非常殘酷的戰爭 。
and these really aggressive behaviors , for the most part , are directed against individuals of the neighboring social group .	這些非常激動的行為 , 大部分部分都在社會群體中 。
they are very territorially aggressive .	它們是非常有力的 。
chimpanzees , i believe , more than any other living creature , have helped us to understand that , after all , there is no sharp line between humans and the rest of the animal kingdom .	黑猩猩 , 我相信 , 比任何其他生物 , 都能幫助我們了解到 , 人類和其他動物王國之間的生物 , 沒有鯊魚 。
it's a very blurry line , and it's getting more blurry all the time as we make even more observations .	這是個非常模糊的線 , 同時 , 我們變得更模糊 , 讓它變得更模糊 。
the study that i began in 1960 is still continuing to this day .	我從1960年開始的研究 , 一直在今日 。
and these chimpanzees , living their complex social lives in the wild , have helped more than anything else to make us realize we are part of , and not separated from , the amazing animals with whom we share the planet .	這些黑猩猩 , 生活在野生動物身上 , 比任何其他東西都能幫助我們 , 讓我們了解到 , 牠們的複雜社會生活在野生動物身上 , 比我們所知的 , 牠們的複雜社會生活在野生動物身上 , 我們都能幫助更多的動物 。
so it's pretty sad to find that chimpanzees , like so many other creatures around the world , are losing their habitats .	所以 , 難以發現黑猩猩 , 像世界上許多其他生物一樣 , 牠們的棲息地被殺害了 。
this is just one photograph from the air , and it shows you the forested highlands of gombe .	這張照片是從空氣中拍攝的 , 它展示給你森林的高溫度 。
and it was when i flew over the whole area , about 16 years ago , and realized that outside the park , this forest , which in 1960 had stretched almost unbroken along the eastern shore of lake tanganyika , which is where the tiny , 30squaremile gombe national park lies , that a question came to my mind .	那時 , 我在1960年 , 到處在公園裡 , 在那裡 , 大約十六年前 , 我從公園的角度來看 , 這位於西班牙的海岸 , 一個問題來到我的腦袋裡 , 大約16年前 。
" how can we even try to save these famous chimpanzees , when the people living around the national park are struggling to survive ? "	「 我們要如何拯救這些名黑猩猩 , 當人們生活在國家公園裡 , 那些有名的黑猩猩 ? 」
more people are living there than the land could possibly support .	更多人住在地球上 , 比土地上有更多人都活著 。
the numbers increased by refugees pouring in from burundi and over the lake from congo .	數量增加 , 來自於難民 , 由難民受難民的苦難 , 來自於難民 。
and very poor people they couldn't afford to buy food from elsewhere .	貧窮的人都無法買食物 。
this led to a program , which we call tacare .	我們稱之為 「 計劃 」 。
it's a very holistic way of improving the lives of the people living in the villages around the park .	這是一種非常有效的方法 , 讓人們生活在公園裡 。
it started small with 12 villages . it's now in 24 .	它從12個村莊開始 , 現在已經24歲了 。
there isn't time to go into it , but it's including things like tree nurseries , methods of farming most suitable to this now very degraded , almost desertlike land up in these mountains .	沒有時間來到它 , 但它包含了很多東西 , 像是樹木工廠 , 幾乎在這些山上 , 幾乎沙漠的土地上 。
ways of controlling , preventing soil erosion .	控制 , 控制、防止土壤 。
ways of reclaiming overused farmland , so that within two years they can again be productive .	再次重複使用農地 , 兩年後 , 牠們可以再次生產力 。
working to help the villagers obtain fresh water from wells .	為了幫助村民的村莊 , 來協助村民的村莊 , 來幫助村民的水源 。
perhaps build some schoolrooms .	或許建造一些學校 。
most important of all , i believe , is working with small groups of women , providing them with opportunities for microcredit loans .	最重要的是 , 我相信 , 和小群女性合作 , 提供他們機會 , 為微信貸款 。
and we've got , as is the case around the world , about 95 percent of all loans returned .	我們已經發現了 , 全世界大約有95%的貸款回收 。
empowering women , working with education , providing scholarships for girls so they can finish secondary school , in the clear understanding that , all around the world , as women's education improves , family size drops .	賦予女性教育的教育 , 提供獎學金給女孩們 , 她們可以完成第二個學校 , 讓女性教育改善和教育 , 讓女性教育改善 , 讓女性教育改善 , 讓女性教育改善 , 讓女性教育改善 , 讓女性教育改善 。
we provide information about family planning and about hiv/aids .	我們提供關於家庭計劃和愛滋病的資訊 。
and as a result of this program , something's happening for conservation .	這種計畫的結果 , 事情會發生在保守 。
what's happening for conservation is that the farmers living in these 24 villages , instead of looking on us as a bunch of white people coming to study a whole bunch of monkeys and by the way , many of the staff are now tanzanian but when we began the tacare program , it was a tanzanian team going into the villages .	對於保育的目標是 , 目前為止 , 我們在24個村莊裡工作 , 不是看著我們 , 如同一群白人人來研究一群大小的農夫 , 如同一群白人 , 來研究一群大小的農夫 , 如同一群白人人來研究一大堆猴子 , 而不是把我們視為一群白人 , 來研究一群大小的農夫 , 如同一群白人 , 來研究一群大小的農夫 , 而不是當我們開始工作時 , 它是坦尚尼亞人 。
it was a tanzanian team talking to the villagers , asking what they were interested in .	這是坦尚尼亞的團隊 , 問他們對他們有什麼興趣 。
were they interested in conservation ? absolutely not .	他們對保育有興趣嗎 ? 絕對不是 。
they were interested in health ; they were interested in education .	他們對健康有興趣 , 他們對教育有興趣 。
and as time went on , and as their situation began to improve , they began to understand ever more about the need for conservation .	隨著時間 , 隨著時間開始改善 , 他們開始了解更多關於保育的需求 。
they began to understand that as the upper levels of the hills were denuded of trees , so you've got this terrible soil erosion and mudslides .	他們開始了解到樹木的土壤和泥土 , 所以你有這種可怕的土壤和泥土 。
today , we are developing what we call the greater gombe ecosystem .	現今 , 我們正在開發我們所謂的 「 更大的生態系統 」 。
this is an area way outside the national park , stretching out into all these very degraded lands .	這是美國國家公園的土地 , 把這些非常殘酷的土地丟出來 。
and as these villages have a better standard of life , they are actually agreeing to put between 10 percent and 20 percent of their land in the highlands aside , so that once again , as the trees grow back , the chimpanzees will have leafy corridors through which they can travel to interact as they must for genetic viability with other remnant groups outside the national park .	當這些村莊有更好的標準時 , 他們的確要在國公園裡有一百分之十的壽命 , 儘管這些村莊有更好的標準 , 一旦這些村莊有更好的標準 , 他們就必須再次重建一群人 , 再次 , 樹木在公園裡 , 再次再次再一次地 , 再一次地 , 樹木在公園裡的樹枝上 , 樹木再次成長 。
so tacare is a success .	任務是成功的 。
we're replicating it in other parts of africa , around other wilderness areas which are faced with extreme population pressure .	我們在非洲其他地方 , 與極端的人口壓抑制度 。
the problems in africa , however , as we've been discussing for the whole of these first couple of days of ted , are major problems .	然而 , 在非洲的幾天 , 我們已經討論了 , 大部分的問題都是主要的問題 。
there is a great deal of poverty .	貧窮的貧窮很大 。
and when you get large numbers of people living in land that is not that fertile , particularly when you cut down trees , and you leave the soil open to the wind for erosion , as desperate populations cut down more and more trees , so that they can try and grow food for themselves and their families , what's going to happen ? something's got to give .	當人們在土地上有更多的樹木 , 你就要離開土壤開放 , 特別是當你砍下樹木時 , 人們會在土壤開放 , 特別是當你砍下樹木時 , 人們會在土壤開放 , 特別是當你把樹木放下去 , 人們會怎麼做 ? 有些事情會發生什麼事 ?
and the other problems in not only africa , but the rest of the developing world and , indeed , everywhere what are we doing to our planet ?	而其他的問題不僅僅是非洲 , 而是全世界的其他問題 , 都在於我們在地球上所做的事 ?
you know , the famous scientist , e . o . wilson said that if every person on this planet attains the standard of living of the average european or american , we need three new planets .	大家都知道 , 美國人 , 我們需要三個新星球 。
today , they are saying four . but we don't have them . we've got one .	今天 , 他們說四個 , 但我們沒有他們 , 我們有了 。
and what's happened ? i mean , the question here is , here we are , arguably the most intelligent being that's ever walked planet earth , with this extraordinary brain , capable of the kind of technology that is so well illustrated by these ted conferences , and yet we're destroying the only home we have .	問題是 , 我是說 , 這裡我們要問的是 , 我們是誰 ? 我是說 , 這裡 , 我們最聰明的 , 是我們最聰明的 , 那些ted會議員工 , 並且我們還能用這些ted會議來做 , 而我們還沒辦法過世了 。
the indigenous people around the world , before they made a major decision , used to sit around and ask themselves , " how does this decision affect our people seven generations ahead ? "	世界各地的人 , 他們做了一個主要決策 , 問自己: 「 這決定如何影響我們七世代的人 ? 」
today , major decisions and i'm not particularly talking about africa here , but the developed world major decisions involving millions of dollars , and millions of people , are often based on , " how will this affect the next shareholders' meeting ? "	今天 , 主要的決策 , 不是特別在談論非洲 , 而是開發中國家主要的決定 , 數百萬人 , 主要的決策是: 「 如何影響下一個共享者的會議 ? 」
and these decisions affect africa .	這些決策會影響非洲 。
as i began traveling around africa talking about the problems faced by chimpanzees and their vanishing forests , i realized more and more how so many of africa's problems could be laid at the door of previous colonial exploitation .	當我開始在非洲各地談談這些問題時 , 我意識到更多 , 許多非洲人的問題都能在非洲的農場上 , 來談談這些問題 。
so i began traveling outside africa , talking in europe , talking in the united states , going to asia .	所以 , 我開始旅行 , 談到歐洲 , 談到歐洲 , 談到歐洲 , 談到歐洲 , 談到歐洲 , 談到歐洲 , 談到歐洲 , 談到美國 。
and everywhere there were these terrible problems .	每處都有這些可怕的問題 。
and you know the kind i'm talking about . i'm talking about pollution .	你們知道我在說的是污染 。
the air that we breathe that often poisons us .	我們呼吸的空氣 , 我們呼吸的空氣 。
the earth is poisoning our foods .	地球是我們的食物 。
the water water is perhaps one of the most crucial issues that we're going to face in this century and everywhere water is being polluted by agricultural , industrial and household chemicals that still are being sprayed around the world , seemingly with the inability to profit from past experience .	水水是最關鍵的問題 , 我們要面對這個世紀 , 和家鄉的農業、工業和農業、工業和家庭化學物質 , 都被污染在這個世紀中 , 卻被污染了 , 幾乎是從過去的經驗中被污染的 。
the mangroves are being cut down ; the effects of things like the tsunami get worse .	溫柔的效果會被降低 , 像海嘯更糟糕的情況 。
we've talked about the soil erosion .	我們談到土壤的土壤 。
we have the reckless burning of fossil fuels along with other greenhouse gasses , so called , leading to climate change .	我們有一堆石油燃料和其他溫室氣候變遷 , 所以我們稱之為氣候變遷 。
finally , all around the world , people have begun to believe that there is something going on very wrong with our climate .	最後 , 在世界各地 , 人們都相信 , 我們的氣候有很大的影響 。
all around the world climates are mixed up .	全世界的氣候都混合了 。
and it's the poor people who are affected worse .	貧窮的人會受到影響更糟糕 。
it's africa that already is affected .	非洲已經被影響了 。
in many parts of subsaharan africa , the droughts are so much worse .	在撒哈拉南非洲的地區 , 乾旱變得更糟糕 。
and when the rain does come , it so often leads to flooding and added distress , and the cycle of poverty and hunger and disease .	當雨林會發生時 , 它通常會導致洪水、飢餓和疾病 。
and the numbers of people living in an area that the land cannot support , who are too poor to buy food , who can't move away because the whole land is degraded .	人口住在土地上 , 土地的數量都不夠窮 , 因為整個土地都被剝奪了 。
and so you get desertification creeping , creeping , creeping as the last of the trees are cut down .	所以 , 你得到沙漠化的回應 , 再次被砍掉 。
and this kind of thing is not just in africa . it's all over the world .	這類東西不僅僅在非洲 , 而是世界各地 。
so it wasn't surprising to me that as i was traveling around the world i met so many young people who seemed to have lost hope .	所以對我來說 , 我遇見了許多年輕人 , 似乎失去希望 。
we seem to have lost wisdom , the wisdom of the indigenous people .	我們似乎失去智慧 , 智慧的智慧 , 智慧的智慧 。
i asked a question . " why ? "	我問一個問題: 「 為什麼 ? 」
well , do you think there could be some kind of disconnect between this extraordinarily clever brain , the kind of brain that the ted technologies exemplify , and the human heart ? talking about it in the nonscientific term , in terms of love and compassion . is there some disconnect ?	你認為 , 人類心臟在非科學領域中有一些不同分裂的大腦 , 人類的心臟在非科學領域 , 與同情心有關 , 與同情心有關 , 與同情心有關 , 人類心臟在哪裡 ?
and these young people , when i talk to them , basically they were either depressed or apathetic , or bitter and angry . and they said more or less the same thing , " we feel this way because we feel you've compromised our future and there's nothing we can do about it . "	這些年輕人 , 當我跟他們說話時 , 基本上 , 他們說: 「 我們感受到 , 基本上 , 基本上 , 基本上 , 基本上 , 基本上 , 基本上 , 基本上是沒有人能做的事 。 」
we have compromised their future .	我們已經承諾了他們的未來 。
i've got three little grandchildren , and every time i look at them and i think how we've harmed this beautiful planet since i was their age , i feel this desperation .	我有三個小孫子 , 每次我看著他們 , 我覺得這個美麗的行星 , 每次我看到這些美麗的星球時 , 我覺得這個美麗的行星 。
and that led to this program we call roots and shoots , which began right here in tanzania and has now spread to 97 countries around the world .	我們稱之為 「 羅根 」 和 「 根源 」 , 開始在坦尚尼亞 , 開始在坦尚尼亞 , 開始在坦尚尼亞 , 到97個國家 。
it's symbolic . roots make a firm foundation .	它是符合的基礎 。 羅根斯為基礎建構 。
shoots seem tiny ; to reach the sun they can break through a brick wall .	射光看起來很小 , 讓太陽能在磚牆上打破 。

hundreds and thousands of young people around the world can break through and can make this a better world for all living things .	全世界有數千名年輕人在世界各地都可以打破 , 讓這個更好的世界 , 能讓世界變得更好 。

the roots and shoots groups all choose three projects .	根根和根根和射擊團隊都選擇三個計畫 。
it depends on how old they are , and which country , whether they're in a city or rural , as to what kinds of projects .	它依舊在城市或鄉村 , 不論是城市或鄉村 , 不管他們是哪個國家 , 不管他們是哪個國家 , 不論是哪個城市或鄉村 。

and every group chooses , between them , three different kinds of project to make this a better world , recognizing that all these different problems are interconnected and impinge on each other .	每一組選擇 , 兩種不同的問題都互相互相連結 , 並將這些不同的問題結合在一起 。

and then , if they're able , they may raise money to help communities in other parts of the world .	然後 , 如果他們能幫助社區 , 他們就能幫助社區在世界各地的其他地方 。
one of their projects will be to help animals not just wildlife , domestic animals as well .	其中一項計畫是幫助動物 , 不只是野生動物 。

and woven throughout all of this is a message of learning to live in peace and harmony within ourselves , in our families , in our communities , between nations , between cultures , between religions and between us and the natural world .	在這兩者之間 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 , 在我們的家庭中 ,

just picking one or two of the projects right here in africa that the roots and shoots groups are doing , one or two projects only in tanzania , in uganda , kenya , south africa , congobrazzaville , sierra leone , cameroon and other groups . and as i say , it's in 97 countries around the world .	舉個例子 , 在烏干達、肯亞、南非、阿拉伯拉、阿拉伯拉、阿拉伯拉、阿拉伯拉、阿拉伯拉、阿拉伯拉、阿拉伯拉、阿拉伯拉、阿拉伯拉、西班牙 , 和其他群體合作 , 我說 , 世界上有九十七個國家的計畫 。

it's being used in uganda to give some psychological help to exchild soldiers .	它在烏干達提供一些心理幫助 , 來幫助給一些心理幫助 。

artist dianna cohen shares some tough truths about plastic pollution in the ocean and in our lives and some thoughts on how to free ourselves from the plastic gyre .	藝術家 , 來自塑膠袋裡的真相 , 來自塑膠污染的真相 , 我們的生活和一些思想 , 讓自己從塑膠污染中消失 。
consumerism , global issues , green , mission blue , oceans , plastic	消費者主義、全球議題、綠色、海洋、塑膠 。
dianna cohen: tough truths about plastic pollution	丹娜•柯蒂:真相對塑膠污染的真相 。
i'm a visual artist , and i'm also one of the cofounders of the plastic pollution coalition .	我是個視覺藝術家 , 我也是其中一個視覺藝術家 。
i've been working with plastic bags , which i cut up and sew back together as my primary material for my artwork for the last 20 years .	我和塑膠袋一起工作 , 把我帶回來的材料 , 用塑膠袋 , 把我帶回到過去二十年間 。
i turn them into two and threedimensional pieces and sculptures and installations .	我把它們放到兩個、三維空間、雕塑和雕塑中 。
upon working with the plastic , after about the first eight years , some of my work started to fissure and break down into smaller little bits of plastic .	大約在八年後 , 我的工作開始分裂 , 小小的塑膠 , 有點塑膠 。
and i thought , " great .	我心想: 「 很棒 。
it's ephemeral just like us . "	就像我們一樣 。 」
upon educating myself a little further about plastics , i actually realized this was a bad thing .	讓我更進一步 , 我了解到這是個壞事 。
it's a bad thing that plastic breaks down into smaller little bits , because it's always still plastic .	塑膠是塑膠碎片 , 因為它總是有塑膠 。
and what we're finding is that a lot of it is in the marine environment .	我們發現的是 , 在海洋環境中 , 許多人都在海洋環境 。
i then , in the last few years , learned about the pacific garbage patch and the gyre .	在過去幾年 , 我發現了太平洋垃圾桶和garbagepatch和garbagepatch和garbagepatch 。
and my initial reaction and i think this is a lot of people's first reaction to learning about it is , " oh my god !	而我的第一個反應就是: 「 喔 ! 我的天啊 !
we've got to go out there and clean this thing up . "	我們必須去清潔這個東西 。 」
so i actually developed a proposal to go out with a cargo ship and two decommissioned fishing trawlers , a crane , a chipping machine and a coldmolding machine .	所以 , 我真的開發了一台機器 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 , 一艘船 。
and my intention was to go out to the gyre , raise awareness about this issue and begin to pick up the plastic , chip it into little bits and cold mold it into bricks that could potentially be used as building materials in underdeveloped communities .	我的意願是 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊上 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊上 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊上 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊上 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊上 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊上 , 把塑膠帶進去 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊上 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊上 , 把塑膠帶進磚塊上 , 讓它變得更小 。
i began talking with people who actually had been out to the gyre and were studying the plastic problem in the marine environment and upon doing so , i realized actually that cleaning it up would be a very small drop in the bucket relative to how much is being generated every day around the world , and that actually i needed to back up and look at the bigger picture .	我開始跟大家說 , 實際上 , 我意識到 , 在海洋環境中 , 我意識到 , 實際上 , 我意識到 , 實際上我需要回來 , 去看大型的塑膠問題 , 實際上我需要回來 , 去看看大型的圖片 。
and the bigger picture is: we need to find a way to turn off the faucet .	更大的圖片是:我們需要找到一種方法 , 來改善 。
we need to cut the spigot of singleuse and disposable plastics , which are entering the marine environment every day on a global scale .	我們需要切割清單、可塑性的塑膠 , 每天都在全球性的塑膠中 , 進入海洋環境 。
so in looking at that , i also realized that i was really angry .	所以 , 我也了解到我很生氣 。

phyllis rodriguez and aicha elwafi have a powerful friendship born of unthinkable loss . rodriguez' son was killed in the world trade center attacks on september 11 , 2001 ; elwafi's son zacarias moussaoui was convicted of a role in those attacks and is serving a life sentence . in hoping to find peace , these two moms have come to understand and respect one another .	羅德里•羅德里•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里斯•羅德里德里茲

i first learned that my son had been in the world trade center on the morning of september 11th , 2001 .	我早上早上9月11日 , 2001年9月11日 , 我發現我兒子在世界貿易中心 。

and when i saw it and yet , through the shock , the terrible shock , and the terrible explosion in our lives , literally , we were not vengeful .	當我看到它時 , 很恐怖的震驚 , 恐怖的震撼 , 是我們生命中最糟糕的爆炸 , 卻是不可思議的 。
and a couple of weeks later when zacarias moussaoui was indicted on six counts of conspiracy to commit terrorism , and the u . s . government called for a death penalty for him , if convicted , my husband and i spoke out in opposition to that , publicly .	幾週後 , 當zacariasmoussaoui被判斷出一個死刑的案例時 , 美國政府稱之為 「 死亡刑事 」 , 而美國政府稱之為 「 死亡刑事 」 , 為他 , 我丈夫 , 和我的丈夫 , 和美國政府打電話給他 。

the smallest bacteria is about 200 nanometers .	最小的細菌是200奈米 。
so a 200nanometer bacteria is going to get through a 200nanometer hole .	所以200奈米的細菌會進入200奈米的細菌 。

so that's definitely going to get through those 200 nanometer holes .	所以 , 這絕對是有限於兩百奈米的洞 。
lifesaver pores are 15 nanometers .	生活品質是15奈米 。
so nothing is getting through .	所以 , 一切都沒辦法通過 。

there's a poem written by a very famous english poet at the end of the 19th century .	在19世紀末期的英文詩人寫了一首詩詞 。
it was said to echo in churchill's brain in the 1930s .	在1930年代 , 教科爾的大腦在1930年代 。
and the poem goes: " on the idle hill of summer , lazy with the flow of streams , hark i hear a distant drummer , drumming like a sound in dreams , far and near and low and louder on the roads of earth go by , dear to friend and food to powder , soldiers marching , soon to die . "	詩人會說: 「 在夏天 , 我聽到一個很遙遠的聲音 , 很快地 , 死了 。 」
those who are interested in poetry , the poem is " a shropshire lad " written by a . e . housman .	那些對詩有興趣的人 , 詩是 「 詩人 」 , 詩是 「 詩人 」 , 詩是 「 詩人 」 的詩詞 。
but what housman understood , and you hear it in the symphonies of nielsen too , was that the long , hot , silvan summers of stability of the 19th century were coming to a close , and that we were about to move into one of those terrifying periods of history when power changes .	但在伊斯蘭人 , 你聽過這句話 , 很久 , 很久 , 熱情 , 二十世紀的歷史上 , 那些很長的一段時間 , 很久 , 很久 , 很久 , 我們就要進入一個很長的一段時間 , 來到我們身邊的歷史 。
and these are always periods , ladies and gentlemen , accompanied by turbulence , and all too often by blood .	這些人常常常常見到血液 。

and these are and we see it very clearly today nearly always highly turbulent times , highly difficult times , and all too often very bloody times .	這些是我們現在看到的 , 非常顯然的 , 通常是非常顯然的 , 非常顯然的 , 通常是非常顯然的 。

and of course , into the vacuum where the tooold european powers used to be were played the two bloody catastrophes of the last century the one in the first part and the one in the second part: the two great world wars .	當然 , 大戰後 , 世界大戰的大戰中 , 二次大戰的大戰中 , 其中一部分是二次大戰 。

we have seen lateral shifts of power the power of greece passed to rome and the power shifts that occurred during the european civilizations but we are seeing something slightly different .	我們在歐洲文明中看到了一些事情 , 在歐洲文明中發生了什麼事 , 但我們看到了一些很不同的東西 。
for power is not just moving laterally from nation to nation .	權力不僅僅僅僅是從國際的角度來看 。
it's also moving vertically .	它也正在移動 。
what's happening today is that the power that was encased , held to accountability , held to the rule of law , within the institution of the nation state has now migrated in very large measure onto the global stage .	現今 , 法律的權力是強大的權力 , 法律的權力 , 被允許在全球階段的權力 。
the globalization of power we talk about the globalization of markets , but actually it's the globalization of real power .	我們談論全球化的全球化 , 但事實上這是全球化的全球化 。
and where , at the nation state level that power is held to accountability subject to the rule of law , on the international stage it is not .	而在國際階段 , 國際階段的規則 , 不管制定法律的規則 。
the international stage and the global stage where power now resides: the power of the internet , the power of the satellite broadcasters , the power of the money changers this vast moneygoround that circulates now 32 times the amount of money necessary for the trade it's supposed to be there to finance the money changers , if you like , the financial speculators that have brought us all to our knees quite recently , the power of the multinational corporations now developing budgets often bigger than mediumsized countries .	國際舞台和全球階段的力量 , 如今 , 金融監控器的力量 , 如今 , 金融監控器的力量 , 如今 , 金融監控器的力量 , 將我們全部的電力轉移到金融監控器 , 將我們全部的電力轉換成金融器 , 將我們推動的電力轉換成金融監控器 , 將我們全部的電力轉換成金融監控器 , 將我們推動的力量 , 轉換為 「 金融資金 」 的力量 , 目前為止 , 金融監控器的力量 , 比美國國際階段的力量更大 。
these live in a global space which is largely unregulated , not subject to the rule of law , and in which people may act free of constraint .	這些生活在一個全球空間中 , 很大的規則 , 不管制定法律的規則 , 不管制定法律的規則 , 人們可能會受到限制的限制 。
now that suits the powerful up to a moment .	現在 , 讓它變得很強大 。

the revelation of 9/11 is that even if you are the most powerful nation on earth , nevertheless , those who inhabit that space can attack you even in your most iconic of cities one bright september morning .	911事件 , 即使你是世界上最強大的國家 , 即使你是地球上最強大的國家 , 甚至是你在地球上最強大的國家 , 即使你是地球上最強大的國家 , 甚至在你最強大的國家中 , 那些住在地球上的人 , 不管你是地球上最強大的國家 。

sooner or later , sooner or later , the rule of history is that where power goes governance must follow .	不久之後 , 歷史的規則是 , 歷史的規則則是 , 權力會持續下去 。

europe in the 19th century: a great british foreign secretary , lord canning , used to describe it as the " european concert of powers . "	歐洲在19世紀:一個偉大的英國外國人 , 叫做 「 歐洲 」 的 「 歐洲 」 。

britain always played to the balance .	英國總是在平衡 。
if paris got together with berlin , britain got together with vienna and rome to provide a counterbalance .	如果巴黎和柏林一起合作 , 英國和柏林一起合作 , 英國和羅馬一起合作 。
now notice , in a period which is dominated by a monopolar world , you have fixed alliances nato , the warsaw pact .	現在 , 注意到 , 在一個月亮世界中 , 你已經有修復的平衡 , 包括 「 伊斯蘭 」 、 「 戰場 」 。
a fixed polarity of power means fixed alliances .	權力的力量意味著解決方案 。

of course they are , they are a mercantilist nation .	當然 , 他們是非國民族群 。

today in our modern world , because of the internet , because of the kinds of things people have been talking about here , everything is connected to everything .	在現代世界裡 , 我們的現代世界 , 因為網路 , 因為網際網路 , 因為網路 , 所有東西都和所有事物有關 。
